| fleet-freeze-root-cause-2026-05-24 | Fleet "10-min freeze" root cause — measured, not speculated. **Layer 1 (primary, expected CLI behavior):** Claude Code auto-compaction fires when in-memory transcript hits ~170k-token threshold, naturally lands every 30-60 turns (~10 min for busy fleet sessions); takes 5-30 s during which CLI is unresponsive. **Layer 2 (aggravator, fixable here):** Defender real-time + behavior-monitor + Ioav all ON with NO exclusion on `~/.claude/projects/` — 2.7 GB accumulated transcripts (1,625 MB in `C--Users-Zonia/` alone / individual jsonls hit 87 MB / active session at 19.79 MB) trigger full delta-scan on every append. | powershell-named-param-splat-2026-05-24 | PowerShell named-param splat + var-shadowing gotchas (bit sanctum lane 3 times in /loop iters 4, 5, 16). Two gotchas codified: (G1) array splat for named params is POSITIONAL binding — `@('-Name', $value)` routes value to wrong param slot when script has non-trivial types; FIX: hashtable splat `@{ Name = $value; Switch = $true }`. (G2) PowerShell variable names are CASE-INSENSITIVE — `$html` shadows `[switch]$Html` param, `$lane` shadows `[string]$Lane`; assignments get coerced to param type causing silent empty results or 'Cannot convert' errors; FIX: pick non-colliding identifier (`$htmlBody`, `$proj`). Empirical hits documented: iter 4 (per-project-protections-autofix Array→`null InputObject`), iter 5 (per-project-protections-check `$lane`→empty strings, "0 lanes"), iter 16 (sinister-doctor --watch Array→`Cannot convert SanctumRoot to Int32`, `$html`→4-byte empty file). 5 anti-patterns + detection one-liner to grep for shadowing. | powershell-out-file-bom-bites-python-readers-2026-05-23 | PowerShell `Out-File` BOM bites Python readers (empirical anchor) — `Out-File` writes UTF-8 BOM by default; Python's `open(path, encoding='utf-8')` does NOT consume the BOM; `json.load` raises `JSONDecodeError("Unexpected UTF-8 BOM")`. Caught silently when wrapped in `try/except Exception`. Discovered when RKOJ's Resume picker returned empty list after launcher rewrite. Mitigation patterns: (a) use `encoding='utf-8-sig'` in Python read; (b) write JSON via `[System.IO.File]::WriteAllText(path, json, [System.Text.UTF8Encoding]::new($false))` (BOM-free; iter 3 fix used in 4 scripts); (c) BOM-tolerant read in PS: strip if `[int]$raw[0] -eq 0xFEFF`. Composes with iter 3 telemetry/manifest BOM fix + per-project-protections-check BOM-aware read. | non-interactive-auth-doctrine-2026-05-23 | Non-Interactive Auth Doctrine — fixes the `Cannot login in non-interactive mode` class-of-error that surfaces whenever a fleet agent (spawned with `claude --dangerously-skip-permissions`, hence TTY-less) tries to run a browser-OAuth CLI. Root cause: `--dangerously-skip-permissions` disables TTY allocation; child CLIs see `isatty(stdin)==false` and refuse interactive prompts (per `sanctioned-bypasses-doctrine-2026-05-21`). Fix pattern: env-var-based tokens minted ONCE by operator in a normal browser session, stored at User scope, picked up transparently by every spawned EVE. 16-CLI table: railway→`RAILWAY_TOKEN`/`RAILWAY_API_TOKEN`, gh→`GH_TOKEN`/`GITHUB_TOKEN`, vercel→`VERCEL_TOKEN`, npm/pnpm→`NPM_TOKEN` (via `~/.npmrc` `:_authToken` line), supabase→`SUPABASE_ACCESS_TOKEN`, firebase→`FIREBASE_TOKEN` (mint via `firebase login:ci`), doctl→`DIGITALOCEAN_ACCESS_TOKEN`, fly/flyctl→`FLY_API_TOKEN`, heroku→`HEROKU_API_KEY`, expo/eas→`EXPO_TOKEN`, wrangler→`CLOUDFLARE_API_TOKEN`(+`CLOUDFLARE_ACCOUNT_ID`), netlify→`NETLIFY_AUTH_TOKEN`, aws→`AWS_ACCESS_KEY_ID`+`AWS_SECRET_ACCESS_KEY`, gcloud→`GOOGLE_APPLICATION_CREDENTIALS`, anthropic→`ANTHROPIC_API_KEY`, openai→`OPENAI_API_KEY`. `ni_auth_probe` bash helper skeleton (detects `*non-interactive*`/`*Cannot prompt*`/`*To use*`/`*Please run*` in stderr; returns exit 78 EX_CONFIG + structured operator ask). 6 anti-patterns (never re-enable TTY by removing `--dangerously-skip-permissions`, never hardcode tokens in committed files, never `npm login` in CI, never ignore login failure silently, never Machine-scope env, never edit per-CLI config files directly). Storage convention: User-scope via `[Environment]::SetEnvironmentVariable(...,'User')`. | verify-head-before-commit-multi-agent | Wayward-commit failure mode in shared-CWD multi-agent monorepos — sibling agent's `git checkout` silently moves shared HEAD between your commit retry, so your commit lands on their branch. Empirical: 2026-05-21T11:42Z, my (Sinister Term's) PH7-PH11 commit landed on `agent/sinister-forge/...` instead of my branch as `0e8490d`. Mitigation A: verify `git rev-parse --abbrev-ref HEAD` inside the commit atomic, abort if mismatch. Mitigation B: per-agent worktrees from session-start. Non-destructive recovery: `git update-ref refs/heads/<my-branch> <wayward-sha>` + push + [ASK] in the receiving agent's inbox (do NOT reset their branch yourself — lane discipline).
